<span key="7991863893d94ac48317ba8f2d79e4ff"><span offset-key="7991863893d94ac48317ba8f2d79e4ff:0">9- Auto-Layout</span></span>

<span key="9af2af3a7fee440cabf30eb067a4a766"><span offset-key="9af2af3a7fee440cabf30eb067a4a766:0">Watch the above .gif to learn this trick.</span></span>

<span key="14402b999ffd4a97811afc3944f7d2b6"><span offset-key="14402b999ffd4a97811afc3944f7d2b6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="0ca92737f38c433f87f9745da44ceb16"></span>

<span key="ea15e91dd6584b21868b6872b6875103"><span offset-key="ea15e91dd6584b21868b6872b6875103:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="84382d6715d542b8945a07718b1dcdbf"></span>

<span key="f3f2fdfc8d80444ca54e7f44e2068d31"><span offset-key="f3f2fdfc8d80444ca54e7f44e2068d31:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="e0c6257cf1884cb3aeb3fe138ad2d012"><span offset-key="e0c6257cf1884cb3aeb3fe138ad2d012:0">Figma was the first design tool which allowed designers to set the space between different elements automatically, It doesn’t matter if the layers are aligned vertically or horizontally!</span></span>

# 

<span key="ab617edad4e149caba13358bc4908a3a"><span offset-key="ab617edad4e149caba13358bc4908a3a:0">8- Define The Space Between Different Elements</span></span>

<span key="e6bf12e8fef34d82ad745d898061c671"><span offset-key="e6bf12e8fef34d82ad745d898061c671:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="3da4078a05c049a5b5cdbcdbadafcb24"></span>

<span key="6f7ce657d2cc442f9219d7787a4efea9"><span offset-key="6f7ce657d2cc442f9219d7787a4efea9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="7ad75e95402645c9b7ad85085690cc5c"></span>

<span key="9e1b23efde34438a9c93fee54187dc3a"><span offset-key="9e1b23efde34438a9c93fee54187dc3a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="c3be9c9fd437489899c03fbd9197df2c"><span offset-key="c3be9c9fd437489899c03fbd9197df2c:0">Hold the “Shift” button and try to draw your desired object. This trick works if you want to draw squares or circles (Not Ovals!).</span></span>

# 

<span key="6c8796b40e4945a5834dfd81d7827e7d"><span offset-key="6c8796b40e4945a5834dfd81d7827e7d:0">7- Create Objects with Equal Height and Width</span></span>

<span key="b24751dc7c364e178dab1bb0a0a89063"><span offset-key="b24751dc7c364e178dab1bb0a0a89063:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="bbabb2b78f0640b8a4c8d4f314fb29c9"></span>

<span key="c283918dfbf84a18a80a97972912ef2f"><span offset-key="c283918dfbf84a18a80a97972912ef2f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="b857e6d61bd6403cb79fe80064e3dc86"></span>

<span key="17922d7fe4f84635929a83444a71f5a1"><span offset-key="17922d7fe4f84635929a83444a71f5a1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="ffe711e633de4c35988d30648540e0c7"><span offset-key="ffe711e633de4c35988d30648540e0c7:0">Follow the below .gif to learn this trick:</span></span>

<span key="41854b1564384160bd79c3ba288baa32"><span offset-key="41854b1564384160bd79c3ba288baa32:0">One of the most important things for designers who work on dashboards or analytical tools is the ability to create semi-circles. Figma allows you to do this easily.</span></span>

# 

<span key="38f8eb0a8fdd4218ae88637d70244654"><span offset-key="38f8eb0a8fdd4218ae88637d70244654:0">6- Create Semi-Circles / Circular Progress Bars</span></span>

<span key="d928be07e85e497eb734a72c5137cec1"><span offset-key="d928be07e85e497eb734a72c5137cec1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="65b65bb5d973472aba63be01e90030b7"></span>

<span key="0f6a277a60594f2aaae307ebccc6f3a7"><span offset-key="0f6a277a60594f2aaae307ebccc6f3a7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="8c8f9ea8b1e84daeb6f1ba0a4f825f0c"></span>

<span key="a48000ca03ec42d68e5e71db85587cdf"><span offset-key="a48000ca03ec42d68e5e71db85587cdf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="403c12e13af0415fb5252ba464eb67b1"><span offset-key="403c12e13af0415fb5252ba464eb67b1:0">There a few plugins for Figma which allow you to find similar layers and apply changes to them. But if you are looking to reduce your usage to 3rd-plugins, you can find similar layers easily by heading to </span>**Edit / Select all …**<span offset-key="403c12e13af0415fb5252ba464eb67b1:2">. There different options which you can use to select similar text styles together or select similar layers with the same properties.</span></span>

# 

<span key="55fc52bfe905474ca84f2134b90bd9ff">**5- Find Similar Layers Without Plugins!**</span>

> <span key="4439038c2636468585667eb1283f00c4"><span offset-key="4439038c2636468585667eb1283f00c4:0">We use same style of naming for colours. For example,</span> **Sort the colors based on their usage:**<span offset-key="4439038c2636468585667eb1283f00c4:2"> Buttons — Blue / Buttons — Red / Alert — Yellow / Texts — Black / Texts- Black (70%)</span></span>

<span key="5079bebb97f9411b9afc9b92467e400d"><span offset-key="5079bebb97f9411b9afc9b92467e400d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="80edeb6326e84b21b7e368f82047b346"></span>

<span key="53b419c9870840ffb79b160d82be0368"><span offset-key="53b419c9870840ffb79b160d82be0368:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span slate-void="true" key="ca177707b464402db3d9d2081f8557eb"></span>

<span key="e1bd948189624f8e93eae0c87f18fbd3"><span offset-key="e1bd948189624f8e93eae0c87f18fbd3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="deb90b9db0bf4c198db2468ab365aa7f"><span offset-key="deb90b9db0bf4c198db2468ab365aa7f:0">and the result would be something like this on Figma:</span></span>

<span key="e7090b9467d84773bdc99d9912a47a1a"><span offset-key="e7090b9467d84773bdc99d9912a47a1a:0">Roboto / Body</span></span>

<span key="c91455899ebc4ddd822d1f45b67d7841"><span offset-key="c91455899ebc4ddd822d1f45b67d7841:0">Roboto / Headline 1</span></span>

<span key="f766a85e01d94beb8e45df017c018c88"><span offset-key="f766a85e01d94beb8e45df017c018c88:0">SF Pro / Body</span></span>

<span key="13dd49dfe9244f08ae1387369ff5464d"><span offset-key="13dd49dfe9244f08ae1387369ff5464d:0">SF Pro / Headline 1</span></span>

<span key="68fb7823a9064cd68079294508e3c29e"><span offset-key="68fb7823a9064cd68079294508e3c29e:0">Now, we want to sort these text styles based on their font family. This is how we do it:</span></span>

<span key="64ff0b17f2ac46c199125cbdc2c57c5d">**Body — 16 px:**<span offset-key="64ff0b17f2ac46c199125cbdc2c57c5d:1"> SF text / Roboto</span></span>

<span key="77cf1375f3934b3da7de6967ec98919a">**Headline 1–36 px :**<span offset-key="77cf1375f3934b3da7de6967ec98919a:1">SF Pro / Roboto</span></span>

<span key="a223bf6370f74d17bd67c84a691b35ec"><span offset-key="a223bf6370f74d17bd67c84a691b35ec:0">Imagine we have these text styles:</span></span>

<span key="f594f041b86145c59a3b2ac507af961d"><span offset-key="f594f041b86145c59a3b2ac507af961d:0">This trick works for designers who think about having a design system or creating a UI kit for their projects. As Sketch does, Figma allows you to sort your text styles by grouping them using “/”.</span></span>

# 

<span key="d09acd30e5304fc88d968a768f8e34c2">**4- Sort Font Styles / Color Styles**</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="47fbb62a4cd74aff95d19914a527dfd1"><span offset-key="47fbb62a4cd74aff95d19914a527dfd1:0">Double-click on the layer’s name will allow you to change the name of the layer!</span></span>

<span key="218174f5d49b4784b5d53afc1e0e22fe"><span offset-key="218174f5d49b4784b5d53afc1e0e22fe:0">If you have worked on a design system, you probably have some problems to find layers. On Figma, you just need to double-click on the layer’s thumbnail to find it:</span></span>

# 

<span key="23051e1b2b7641d58e3009c76dce34e1"><span offset-key="23051e1b2b7641d58e3009c76dce34e1:0">3- Locate Layers</span></span>

<span key="05f4c61e421542c3881b04c1401955e2"><span offset-key="05f4c61e421542c3881b04c1401955e2:0">To move an object easily and on a straight line, just hold “Shift” button on your keyboard and then try to relocate it. By doing this, Figma will limit you to the vertical axis or horizontal axis.</span></span>

<span key="9971a519f4844c08a53277d260bd65e0"><span offset-key="9971a519f4844c08a53277d260bd65e0:0">If you are one of the designers who play with pixels to draw a straight line, you need to learn this trick. Just select the “Pen Tool” or “Line” and hold “Shift” button on your keyboard. Now, you can draw a straight line easily!</span></span>

# 

<span key="c34b03b7a7c8478dacc077397bf8f811"><span offset-key="c34b03b7a7c8478dacc077397bf8f811:0">2- Draw Straight Lines / Move Objects on a Straight Line</span></span>

<span key="7c60c0a5463d4ff48a7835f9f03e2bf0"><span offset-key="7c60c0a5463d4ff48a7835f9f03e2bf0:0">File → Place Images and then select the images. Now, click on the shapes and Figma will fill shapes with images automatically.</span></span>

<span key="c681390a24eb4b038edf7a80e9a69941"><span offset-key="c681390a24eb4b038edf7a80e9a69941:0">Follow these steps:</span></span>

<span key="16aa8553da814952a55337530e3470e9"><span offset-key="16aa8553da814952a55337530e3470e9:0">Imagine you want to fill different shapes with multiple images at once. Beginners will start filling shapes one by one but professionals will use the “Batch Image Import” feature which Figma provides.</span></span>

# 

<span key="4626012fdf034ce4be44353d9fcf18b3"><span offset-key="4626012fdf034ce4be44353d9fcf18b3:0">1- Batch Filling Shapes With Images</span></span>

<span key="0afa2bf1338e43f9aea249493d91cf06"><span offset-key="0afa2bf1338e43f9aea249493d91cf06:0">In this article, we will learn the most useful shortcuts of Figma which can speed up your workflow.</span></span>

<span key="f45db9a3e61c484e9a10e93b05482f83"><span offset-key="f45db9a3e61c484e9a10e93b05482f83:0">Hello again, It’s Em!</span></span>

<span key="90178229e88a4f60bb510a9181165fd8"><span offset-key="90178229e88a4f60bb510a9181165fd8:0">Figma is one of the amazing design tools and if you use it as your daily design app, you need to learn its shortcuts which speeds up your workflow.</span></span>

<span key="a3a6dbdf419d499086bc46200283e659"><span offset-key="a3a6dbdf419d499086bc46200283e659:0">Introduction</span></span>

<span key="98146823744a4764973aa5d71cade5da"><span offset-key="98146823744a4764973aa5d71cade5da:0">Welcome to Figma, the world's first collaborative interface design tool. Figma allows designers to create and prototype their digital experiences - together in real-time and in one place - helping them turn their ideas and visions into products, faster. Figma's mission is to make design accessible to everyone. The Figma API is one of the ways we aim to do that.What can I do with the Figma API?</span></span>

<span key="1d1547ad466746e28d67a78a7301cd4c"><span offset-key="1d1547ad466746e28d67a78a7301cd4c:0">The Figma API supports read access and interactions with Figma files. This gives you the ability to view and extract any objects or layers, and their properties, so you can render them as images outside of Figma. You can then present your designs, connect them to other applications, or use them to expand on your vision. Future versions of the API will unlock even greater functionality around Files.How does it work?</span></span>

<span key="e6145e727a4d4025897ca21d8e81576e"><span offset-key="e6145e727a4d4025897ca21d8e81576e:0">The Figma API is based on the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Representational_state_transfer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="df1f2c55dafa44aeb3a0f87400ae75fe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="79299459dc514604bc11c93458a48488"><span data-offset-key="79299459dc514604bc11c93458a48488:0">REST</span></span></span></a><span key="bd0343b4223741eeaa6a2bec0166eb82"><span offset-key="bd0343b4223741eeaa6a2bec0166eb82:0"> structure. We support authentication via </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#access-tokens" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d2c28a2e316548c58814e74603482cc3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="0495a1fb0904460fa1e16d7128144634"><span data-offset-key="0495a1fb0904460fa1e16d7128144634:0">access tokens</span></span></span></a><span key="8fa75bda42e147ea9940bc4ee521247b"><span offset-key="8fa75bda42e147ea9940bc4ee521247b:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#oauth2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3e0eca2e7b2f41739cdb9f9f48e1a3fe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="3b3ddef781cd4e6db48ff6bb313e5b16"><span data-offset-key="3b3ddef781cd4e6db48ff6bb313e5b16:0">OAuth2</span></span></span></a><span key="8e07456f03b14f5298eb9d9ab21038e8"><span offset-key="8e07456f03b14f5298eb9d9ab21038e8:0">. Requests are made via HTTP endpoints with clear functions and appropriate response codes. Endpoints allow you to request </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#files" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7f033f4ffcab4b3b90f6435bc59eedc5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="537a4d40b017459da2e8701d7e7f330b"><span data-offset-key="537a4d40b017459da2e8701d7e7f330b:0">files</span></span></span></a><span key="8ca34f623ca343829fea2ddea3b999cb"><span offset-key="8ca34f623ca343829fea2ddea3b999cb:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#get-images-endpoint" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8fcba1cd8c634a82b6225d1e861e0157" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="bd7ab1c5a8d54328be2b7cf5f584ab71"><span data-offset-key="bd7ab1c5a8d54328be2b7cf5f584ab71:0">images</span></span></span></a><span key="a15e4970ade54ee6a77bf092c08116aa"><span offset-key="a15e4970ade54ee6a77bf092c08116aa:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#version-history" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7afb55bf1d664b0088eaa162fa11197d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="256c1c08a4314254b593f6855826f8fd"><span data-offset-key="256c1c08a4314254b593f6855826f8fd:0">file versions</span></span></span></a><span key="ba2b75b1391d4d6596ba4b1d24e8e877"><span offset-key="ba2b75b1391d4d6596ba4b1d24e8e877:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#users" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7110bac293904f30ae01205293443e64" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="13c5b6e516cb481ba77c51059ce0cbab"><span data-offset-key="13c5b6e516cb481ba77c51059ce0cbab:0">users</span></span></span></a><span key="2ae2675609b74d78acd2916c927b4b45"><span offset-key="2ae2675609b74d78acd2916c927b4b45:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#comments" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="95f466cf33d549db83249180ef17692c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="15adbafe78f344b7b04e2e67e2d341d9"><span data-offset-key="15adbafe78f344b7b04e2e67e2d341d9:0">comments</span></span></span></a><span key="1291721eb54848d1aba358b818839301"><span offset-key="1291721eb54848d1aba358b818839301:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#get-team-projects-endpoint" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="99a62cb6835b4e5fae03357ca2660069" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="c2b08e896d3c4015adb2a2a081f993de"><span data-offset-key="c2b08e896d3c4015adb2a2a081f993de:0">team projects</span></span></span></a><span key="4ff6f2cf209c47a3bb9b3dbd485a606c"><span offset-key="4ff6f2cf209c47a3bb9b3dbd485a606c:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#get-project-files-endpoint" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7ec9916ac3aa4dbea9d6ac4b7427a3c4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="5ed92beb96a8438ca9a6998fa72f7c38"><span data-offset-key="5ed92beb96a8438ca9a6998fa72f7c38:0">project files</span></span></span></a><span key="05e6d6fd485a4b28b3ca1f141988992d"><span offset-key="05e6d6fd485a4b28b3ca1f141988992d:0">.</span></span>

<span key="b6ef8dcecc934f57a9669e4870ff731b"><span offset-key="b6ef8dcecc934f57a9669e4870ff731b:0">Once granted access, you can use the Figma API to inspect a JSON representation of the file. Every layer or object in a file will be represented within the file by a node (subtree). You will then be able to access and isolate the object and any properties associated with it. In addition to accessing files and layers, you will be able to GET and POST comments to files.Getting started</span></span>

<span key="08d97beafe614de3ab59e34b39ea6982"><span offset-key="08d97beafe614de3ab59e34b39ea6982:0">If you’re not already using Figma, the first step is to sign up and create an account </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/signup" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ba88bdd62ae14977b5314be1fa281e89" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="673175f97b0545448ea1221a3c022da3"><span data-offset-key="673175f97b0545448ea1221a3c022da3:0">over here.</span></span></span></a><span key="2010400532ff4e25a54af43dfe8033a3"><span offset-key="2010400532ff4e25a54af43dfe8033a3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="ee7438546faa40b2869b222dc6c8791d"><span offset-key="ee7438546faa40b2869b222dc6c8791d:0">Once you have a Figma account, the next step is to authenticate with the API. This can be done using either </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#oauth2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="88a56642aea74a22a1a5e39c0a6ef0ef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="a959600a55f844e3a06241287c1b2c81"><span data-offset-key="a959600a55f844e3a06241287c1b2c81:0">OAuth2</span></span></span></a><span key="f40b3414b94c43fd8e77d3fc4f5d9967"><span offset-key="f40b3414b94c43fd8e77d3fc4f5d9967:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#access-tokens" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cbb88cb99521487eb2cfe4c9044f2dfe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="002bd39207114fc482d5411c1001e7df"><span data-offset-key="002bd39207114fc482d5411c1001e7df:0">access tokens</span></span></span></a><span key="1a6fbc29eb1d413baa6738a03b69b579"><span offset-key="1a6fbc29eb1d413baa6738a03b69b579:0">.</span></span>

<span key="6cb9e191ba574029af7f1cd48eccc242"><span offset-key="6cb9e191ba574029af7f1cd48eccc242:0">You can then browse our endpoints and start making queries against the Figma API. We recommend starting with the basics by learning about </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#files" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="837015329c04445c984565aede4d0331" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="948d59d46e6d4d8597c89ac6f9b4e640"><span data-offset-key="948d59d46e6d4d8597c89ac6f9b4e640:0">Figma files</span></span></span></a><span key="796d869a6af747c883736ef8714d9755"><span offset-key="796d869a6af747c883736ef8714d9755:0">, before moving on to more advanced topics such as </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#comments" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7e05be54c40047cba4a93fd68d95528a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="ae71b4a6d6ac4963910e148bedd9cbc5"><span data-offset-key="ae71b4a6d6ac4963910e148bedd9cbc5:0">comments</span></span></span></a><span key="00321f98e4494345a181f35b8c80f070"><span offset-key="00321f98e4494345a181f35b8c80f070:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#users" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5f003a0f39fd4d76a809f05aa53e3037" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="02c037ccc17b47f89aee7a708a60befb"><span data-offset-key="02c037ccc17b47f89aee7a708a60befb:0">users</span></span></span></a><span key="d0c18eeb04e14e11a2f808f2a5f215db"><span offset-key="d0c18eeb04e14e11a2f808f2a5f215db:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#version-history" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fb7190d17cd94e9eb1cbcfde9c43bc44" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="eac0aa280c9443218ce0dc945a35d7d8"><span data-offset-key="eac0aa280c9443218ce0dc945a35d7d8:0">version history</span></span></span></a><span key="6368bffd85b647398f7ba14a3d2e1e57"><span offset-key="6368bffd85b647398f7ba14a3d2e1e57:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#projects" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b7071f8cc3ed4d50865ff495882518a7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="d9a7055427e644d49d1195302322fa72"><span data-offset-key="d9a7055427e644d49d1195302322fa72:0">projects</span></span></span></a><span key="e4c20969b106453daae6c0832fefa423"><span offset-key="e4c20969b106453daae6c0832fefa423:0">.</span></span>

<span key="fe1225324d3040698b1075123c340fba"><span offset-key="fe1225324d3040698b1075123c340fba:0">If you plan on building a fully-fledged app, that others can share and use, then you can register your app by heading to </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/apps" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="aaaa5049c71641409e2803b7edd2392e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="c4721f548f2545ccb168f13b8e141ea8"><span data-offset-key="c4721f548f2545ccb168f13b8e141ea8:0">My apps</span></span></span></a><span key="018163e147fd46809489a25d5364fa76"><span offset-key="018163e147fd46809489a25d5364fa76:0"> in your Figma account.Base URLhttps://api.figma.comAuthentication</span></span>

<span key="616975efabc6433b835717892c5a55ef"><span offset-key="616975efabc6433b835717892c5a55ef:0">Before you can access an endpoint within Figma, you will need to provide valid authentication. You can authenticate your request to the Figma API in two ways:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="bc9a3d0adec9426b99f99119d99d9f14"><span offset-key="bc9a3d0adec9426b99f99119d99d9f14:0">Generate a personal access token through your user profile page. This gives you access to the Figma API as if you were a single user.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="a465de61b75b4c62b060102ebf24f228"><span offset-key="a465de61b75b4c62b060102ebf24f228:0">Recommended: register a callback via OAuth2 and collect a client secret. This allows you non-specific access to the Figma API, without having to act on behalf of a specific user.</span></span>

<span key="f7c2868a3b284ce19507e7eea0ffbc94"><span offset-key="f7c2868a3b284ce19507e7eea0ffbc94:0">Access tokensA personal access token gives the holder access to an account through the API as if they were the user who generated the token.Generate a personal access token</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="6ca371847ca048b3b26995c69d60894a"><span offset-key="6ca371847ca048b3b26995c69d60894a:0">Login to your Figma account.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="f061bcb4ad674d88b14537620977b889"><span offset-key="f061bcb4ad674d88b14537620977b889:0">Head to the account settings from the top-left menu inside Figma.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="9fa96cebddf44eab9a683a8e36aee7c5"><span offset-key="9fa96cebddf44eab9a683a8e36aee7c5:0">Find the personal access tokens section.</span></span>

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
    <span key="b7b0c4d63e9741b08ca46ef4fccb5842"><span offset-key="b7b0c4d63e9741b08ca46ef4fccb5842:0">Click Create new token.</span></span>

5.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">5.</span>
    <span key="5502a293f2f44335a113697612bca7a7"><span offset-key="5502a293f2f44335a113697612bca7a7:0">A token will be generated. This will be your only chance to copy the token, so make sure you keep a copy of this in a secure place.</span></span>

<span key="152fecb2531d483da2d51fba2ab1c266"><span offset-key="152fecb2531d483da2d51fba2ab1c266:0">From the account settings page, you will also be able to see when the token was last used (give or take a few minutes). If you see any activity on a token that you did not initiate, revoke the token immediately. Revocations are instant and can be made at any time.</span></span>

<span key="f91bcf7861404fa19b09e558230e32f5"><span offset-key="f91bcf7861404fa19b09e558230e32f5:0">You can also generate an access token from this page to explore our endpoints. The token generated here functions exactly the same as a token generated from the account settings page as in the instructions above.Use the personal access token</span></span>

<span key="4d5a270757934b3db459012b22515087"><span offset-key="4d5a270757934b3db459012b22515087:0">You can now use the token to make requests to the Figma API. You can do so by passing the token to the API in the header of your request. We’ve shown you an example of how this would look.</span></span>

<span key="6a52a6626b4946a5b67396f8bda5e4b9"><span offset-key="6a52a6626b4946a5b67396f8bda5e4b9:0">The name of the token header is X-Figma-Token.+ Get personal access token</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#access-tokens" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d8754e94472c4a52afba0cc49d7dcf05" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="6a7144a2c9624ccab6e4a258f4482814"><span data-offset-key="6a7144a2c9624ccab6e4a258f4482814:0">What's this?</span></span></span></a><span key="2168f397b05f4ea4beab4a0781e8fb52"><span offset-key="2168f397b05f4ea4beab4a0781e8fb52:0">Using the token to make requests</span></span>

1

Copied!

<span key="dc737769b4d2400e921f083fe328f605"><span offset-key="dc737769b4d2400e921f083fe328f605:0">OAuth 2</span></span><a href="https://oauth.net/2/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ddf66ceccaca444da598f0d74a60e9dc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="4f8948ffac614625a75d81a51587b879"><span data-offset-key="4f8948ffac614625a75d81a51587b879:0">OAuth 2</span></span></span></a><span key="ad117884a4b44590bd5ec5cd03378ffc"><span offset-key="ad117884a4b44590bd5ec5cd03378ffc:0"> is a web security protocol that allows 3rd party applications to establish a link between a user’s account and their access to a given API, on behalf of that user. We support OAuth 2 authentication in addition to personal access tokens. You would use OAuth 2 when you would like to access the Figma API, without having to identify yourself as a specific user.</span></span>

<span key="e45e643d51034652a6fff891912f6321"><span offset-key="e45e643d51034652a6fff891912f6321:0">To get started with OAuth 2:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="2acf56d5a0ee4876a9bf76d42928cfe8"><span offset-key="2acf56d5a0ee4876a9bf76d42928cfe8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#register-oauth2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="194409917f4f43c280abeaf53e834b0b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="2cdfd0d732d54d908d36304382ffe7cd"><span data-offset-key="2cdfd0d732d54d908d36304382ffe7cd:0">Register an application via your Figma account.</span></span></span></a><span key="92c47de2eab24aeb81c2bfb7b9d68767"><span offset-key="92c47de2eab24aeb81c2bfb7b9d68767:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="60431f7eca594a6ebc6ea9aa39ce3a72"><span offset-key="60431f7eca594a6ebc6ea9aa39ce3a72:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#auth-oauth2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="763f68ac171944509fa5ca4655ae2aa3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="3fa1b2961fdb43a78d77d625c9ee3bb6"><span data-offset-key="3fa1b2961fdb43a78d77d625c9ee3bb6:0">Authenticate any users.</span></span></span></a><span key="45c50674f64841abafebcedc17af5ac6"><span offset-key="45c50674f64841abafebcedc17af5ac6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="40ee3852e0a64f18917fe2c21a47df5c"><span offset-key="40ee3852e0a64f18917fe2c21a47df5c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#token-oauth2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5ec4da4d52d34570839174a74d5a3aba" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="e598dccd6b4c4f76bfd187f5ad27b6aa"><span data-offset-key="e598dccd6b4c4f76bfd187f5ad27b6aa:0">Use the OAuth 2 Token.</span></span></span></a><span key="56beb08a405543d3b22513f1a27e197f"><span offset-key="56beb08a405543d3b22513f1a27e197f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
    <span key="e67fb4cad5f44ee9abcbf94d091b5c3c"><span offset-key="e67fb4cad5f44ee9abcbf94d091b5c3c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#refresh-oauth2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bb75567b3638474189ed51666cf09220" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="d45ba9d979ce402fb83699a6a7b84a9d"><span data-offset-key="d45ba9d979ce402fb83699a6a7b84a9d:0">Refresh an OAuth 2 Token.</span></span></span></a><span key="c95712cd04f2471597b74b26fc43b21b"><span offset-key="c95712cd04f2471597b74b26fc43b21b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="731e001746a147dab41758e8900ecdf2"><span offset-key="731e001746a147dab41758e8900ecdf2:0">Register an Application</span></span>

<span key="7f2981cd22974a7ab8e386ec67a11b29"><span offset-key="7f2981cd22974a7ab8e386ec67a11b29:0">Registering an app establishes a link between your existing Figma user account(s) and your application, which allows you to access data via the Figma API on the user's behalf.</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="3192d77d8dea4d15a952de3cd89be09f"><span offset-key="3192d77d8dea4d15a952de3cd89be09f:0">Head to the </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/apps" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0c01fb174ed24beebd0998a418f891ec" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="b53738e4e03146ac8383eebe70ca5824"><span data-offset-key="b53738e4e03146ac8383eebe70ca5824:0">My apps</span></span></span></a><span key="84af7552c9344bb7a8e89eb420967bfb"><span offset-key="84af7552c9344bb7a8e89eb420967bfb:0"> tab to get started.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="1c892c48fea149c5afdf39a3311f879b"><span offset-key="1c892c48fea149c5afdf39a3311f879b:0">In the Registered apps section, click Create a new app.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="b708728c81644f598738dc8e9bef1d3a"><span offset-key="b708728c81644f598738dc8e9bef1d3a:0">You’ll then need to complete some details about your application:</span></span>

    1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
        <span key="ccd8d2eb675f48058d12a710fd9f8f68"><span offset-key="ccd8d2eb675f48058d12a710fd9f8f68:0">Enter the name and website for your app.</span></span>

    2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
        <span key="fb1e60cfd555478b9ca015b2597e8add"><span offset-key="fb1e60cfd555478b9ca015b2597e8add:0">Upload a logo for your application users will be able to see this).</span></span>

    3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
        <span key="73da01a0d20541b9a44a09c063c0420c"><span offset-key="73da01a0d20541b9a44a09c063c0420c:0">Specify the Callback. This can be any endpoint/URL of your choosing. You must specify at least one callback and only callbacks appearing in this list will be allowed to receive the access token.</span></span>

    4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
        <span key="d6b9dc8ecb974d92b7fb061172627915"><span offset-key="d6b9dc8ecb974d92b7fb061172627915:0">\\</span></span>

    5.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">5.</span>
        <span key="82ece2244fe440018bb05ddcd60fc8f1"><span offset-key="82ece2244fe440018bb05ddcd60fc8f1:0">What is a Callback?</span></span>

    6.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">6.</span>
        <span key="4098d46e45964e2d8ca4ff580e8eb862"><span offset-key="4098d46e45964e2d8ca4ff580e8eb862:0">When a user attempts to allow your application access to the API, our authentication servers will make a request (a Callback) to the endpoint you specified, with the access token included.</span></span>

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
    <span key="cd6c089c1b4b452bb9cacda97ddebe1f"><span offset-key="cd6c089c1b4b452bb9cacda97ddebe1f:0">Click Save to create the app.</span></span>

5.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">5.</span>
    <span key="6222e6e3d716425f98eca69b5d0c4954"><span offset-key="6222e6e3d716425f98eca69b5d0c4954:0">You will be given your client ID and client secret. This will allow you to access the Figma API. The client secret will only be shown to you once! Copy it now and store it someplace safe.</span></span><span slate-void="true" key="08f0dd19a696466c8bdb93f65467f74b"></span>

    <span key="2edc74ff2cd0447cb8b0a8e4ada6ba6b"><span offset-key="2edc74ff2cd0447cb8b0a8e4ada6ba6b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="d619a6432fde41a4a0634a0ef9036ba8"><span offset-key="d619a6432fde41a4a0634a0ef9036ba8:0">You’re now ready to authenticate users via your app!</span></span>

<span key="c4053c9a8494450dac1c52321b762bfa"><span offset-key="c4053c9a8494450dac1c52321b762bfa:0">Authenticate users</span></span>

<span key="c5ffde21c96f446fb4c7b523a91c6e75"><span offset-key="c5ffde21c96f446fb4c7b523a91c6e75:0">To authenticate any users, ask them to visit the following URL:</span></span>

1

<span key="56962f6cc18e4746853b4332ca89cb76"><span offset-key="56962f6cc18e4746853b4332ca89cb76:0">GET https://www.figma.com/oauth?</span></span>

2

<span key="af21443165f64999a3a489d4cf352dad"><span offset-key="af21443165f64999a3a489d4cf352dad:0"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="af21443165f64999a3a489d4cf352dad:1">client\_id</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="af21443165f64999a3a489d4cf352dad:2">=</span><span offset-key="af21443165f64999a3a489d4cf352dad:3">:client\_id</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="af21443165f64999a3a489d4cf352dad:4">&</span></span>

3

<span key="11d64431e22f46cdacc276602d1e0fd1"><span offset-key="11d64431e22f46cdacc276602d1e0fd1:0"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="11d64431e22f46cdacc276602d1e0fd1:1">redirect\_uri</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="11d64431e22f46cdacc276602d1e0fd1:2">=</span><span offset-key="11d64431e22f46cdacc276602d1e0fd1:3">:callback</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="11d64431e22f46cdacc276602d1e0fd1:4">&</span></span>

4

<span key="772cfdb2842a4cf99b25abbd60d7765d"><span offset-key="772cfdb2842a4cf99b25abbd60d7765d:0"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="772cfdb2842a4cf99b25abbd60d7765d:1">scope</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="772cfdb2842a4cf99b25abbd60d7765d:2">=</span><span offset-key="772cfdb2842a4cf99b25abbd60d7765d:3">file\_read</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="772cfdb2842a4cf99b25abbd60d7765d:4">&</span></span>

5

<span key="fa83576d168748c38774176e788af6c1"><span offset-key="fa83576d168748c38774176e788af6c1:0"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fa83576d168748c38774176e788af6c1:1">state</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fa83576d168748c38774176e788af6c1:2">=</span><span offset-key="fa83576d168748c38774176e788af6c1:3">:state</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fa83576d168748c38774176e788af6c1:4">&</span></span>

6

<span key="323dfec36cc045f6a5eaa0c68abc3e61"><span offset-key="323dfec36cc045f6a5eaa0c68abc3e61:0"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="323dfec36cc045f6a5eaa0c68abc3e61:1">response\_type</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="323dfec36cc045f6a5eaa0c68abc3e61:2">=</span><span offset-key="323dfec36cc045f6a5eaa0c68abc3e61:3">code</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0yOTYzXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="d24117926b264b9ca36b405c6e4ed503"><span offset-key="d24117926b264b9ca36b405c6e4ed503:0">Important: this URL must be accessed via the user's browser and not an embedded webview inside your application. Webview access to the Figma OAuth flow is not supported and may stop working for some or all users without an API version update.</span></span>

Parameter

Description

<span key="0e9b819a9ccc4dd2b28bc225eec83f50"><span offset-key="0e9b819a9ccc4dd2b28bc225eec83f50:0">client\_id</span></span>

<span key="f4eb814af92f4e30b18ff520621fe2dd"><span offset-key="f4eb814af92f4e30b18ff520621fe2dd:0">The client ID for your app. In the example Pencil app above, the client ID is fGd5TpaewrbjLdsrGO33AP.</span></span>

<span key="36c477de8c3744e2b9afcb62c526448c"><span offset-key="36c477de8c3744e2b9afcb62c526448c:0">redirect\_uri</span></span>

<span key="bf957119804a4ffbb778e48e0acc17eb"><span offset-key="bf957119804a4ffbb778e48e0acc17eb:0">This must be one of the values you set as your callbacks in the app creation/edit screen. The auth page will call this URI if the user allows access to your app.</span></span>

<span key="f0363ee0ee254ccc8c437e18fdfb8480"><span offset-key="f0363ee0ee254ccc8c437e18fdfb8480:0">scope</span></span>

<span key="fb63f31f3d9a424a9caaedf621208be4"><span offset-key="fb63f31f3d9a424a9caaedf621208be4:0">Currently this value can only be file\_read signifying read-only access to the user's files.</span></span>

<span key="ca689cb0f24a4196a7e6fdba9e590953"><span offset-key="ca689cb0f24a4196a7e6fdba9e590953:0">state</span></span>

<span key="15b8e32529a340cdb34aba1e04044cb5"><span offset-key="15b8e32529a340cdb34aba1e04044cb5:0">This is a value that you should randomly generate and store. When we call back to your callback endpoint, you should check that the state value we pass back to you matches the state value that you initially used in your request.</span></span>

<span key="3b0a0458014742bbbc7e9342ec5fb175"><span offset-key="3b0a0458014742bbbc7e9342ec5fb175:0">response\_type</span></span>

<span key="0fdd30c702fc4d8e810a3bac1bf297e6"><span offset-key="0fdd30c702fc4d8e810a3bac1bf297e6:0">Currently we only support the authorization code flow for OAuth 2, so the only valid value here is code. We may support other values in the future.</span></span>

<span key="f56c81714cb54b1bb0572328b3a6751c"><span offset-key="f56c81714cb54b1bb0572328b3a6751c:0">Once the user navigates to this address, they will see a screen like the following:</span></span><span slate-void="true" key="0e27c95dace143dd964420e69c0ac088"></span>

<span key="81aaf03b309c4fa2be42d27a75906700"><span offset-key="81aaf03b309c4fa2be42d27a75906700:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="2b6afe8fb6cc400faeec7dd96e2a0a0a"><span offset-key="2b6afe8fb6cc400faeec7dd96e2a0a0a:0">If the user rejects the request, no callback is triggered.</span></span>

<span key="194cbbf9f8ee417d8156992044c09cd8"><span offset-key="194cbbf9f8ee417d8156992044c09cd8:0">At this point, the client will be redirected to the callback that was passed as redirect\_uri.If the redirect URI that was provided is https://example.com/oauth/callback, then the expected callback request would look like: https://example.com/oauth/callback?code=:code&state=:state</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="30db84210b5a407db1c946bdea0fd687"><span offset-key="30db84210b5a407db1c946bdea0fd687:0">:code here refers to the authentication code that can be traded in for an access token.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="e85ded4595d242169dd9252c5cccacbc"><span offset-key="e85ded4595d242169dd9252c5cccacbc:0">:state refers to the state variable that was in the initial url given to the user.</span></span>

<span key="596df987a33f41b287092992cd29f06a"><span offset-key="596df987a33f41b287092992cd29f06a:0">Please check that the state parameter passed back to you is the same as the one originally generated.</span></span>

<span key="779e6142130749a4aa5616ed1ca479d1"><span offset-key="779e6142130749a4aa5616ed1ca479d1:0">Now the code can be passed back to the OAuth API to get the user's access token:</span></span>

1

<span key="383e754121c04263b659d5725794a53a"><span offset-key="383e754121c04263b659d5725794a53a:0">POST https://www.figma.com/api/oauth/token?</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="8affaf54b6654d28a7e02cf391e9f895"><span offset-key="8affaf54b6654d28a7e02cf391e9f895:0">:callback must match the redirect URI originally provided, and code must match the authentication code provided to your callback.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7607f841e1c84baba66d7b9658254639"><span offset-key="7607f841e1c84baba66d7b9658254639:0">:client\_secret is the secret key that you copied when you created your application.</span></span>

<span key="7348a925e4894114970ac613665a6c34"><span offset-key="7348a925e4894114970ac613665a6c34:0">If the parameters match, you will receive the user access token and token expiration (in seconds) in a JSON response.Using the OAuth 2 Token</span></span>

<span key="ee145fe741744e13802d83d45542da52"><span offset-key="ee145fe741744e13802d83d45542da52:0">Once you have obtained the user access token, using it is very similar to the way you use </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#access-tokens" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="388711aa5d554f67b73679a20a1ac382" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="4ffa5c85431044d1962174b01121a69e"><span data-offset-key="4ffa5c85431044d1962174b01121a69e:0">personal access tokens.</span></span></span></a><span key="65d62ff27ae1414bbf39b09792e87c0b"><span offset-key="65d62ff27ae1414bbf39b09792e87c0b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="85233f0c710141b9a890cac00d2b93c7"><span offset-key="85233f0c710141b9a890cac00d2b93c7:0">When you call the API, pass a Bearer authorization header like so:</span></span>

1

<span key="e77c0a2de6bd4672911cfbca9be49798"><span offset-key="e77c0a2de6bd4672911cfbca9be49798:0">$ </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77c0a2de6bd4672911cfbca9be49798:1">curl</span><span offset-key="e77c0a2de6bd4672911cfbca9be49798:2"> -sH </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77c0a2de6bd4672911cfbca9be49798:3">'Authorization: Bearer &lt;TOKEN>'</span></span>

2

<span key="caf8423918664c15ba5c5db9f858d0ba"><span offset-key="caf8423918664c15ba5c5db9f858d0ba:0"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="caf8423918664c15ba5c5db9f858d0ba:1">'https://api.figma.com/v1/files/...'</span></span>

<span key="043d99652cdc4a8d94d719635623be84"><span offset-key="043d99652cdc4a8d94d719635623be84:0">Refreshing OAuth tokens</span></span>

<span key="6ef73ec2a1cd4931861f0b3d4f1cd40f"><span offset-key="6ef73ec2a1cd4931861f0b3d4f1cd40f:0">By default OAuth tokens expire after 90 days so you will need to refresh your stored tokens if your integration is long-lived. You do this using the refresh\_token.</span></span>

<span key="897fe9ffe74448e2bd142be30d8d49f6"><span offset-key="897fe9ffe74448e2bd142be30d8d49f6:0">Your refresh\_token can be reused as many times as necessary to retrieve a new access\_token. This requires you to POST a request to refresh the token, based on its current expiry date. Here’s how that looks:</span></span>

1

<span key="b76586768fca42b691ffe08e79138a91"><span offset-key="b76586768fca42b691ffe08e79138a91:0">POST https://www.figma.com/api/oauth/refresh?</span></span>

2

<span key="8a477d58bf3d4e75afb1d506bda3b247"><span offset-key="8a477d58bf3d4e75afb1d506bda3b247:0"> client\_id=:client\_id&</span></span>

3

<span key="5ec932c983fe4ffea18689d0cbd39840"><span offset-key="5ec932c983fe4ffea18689d0cbd39840:0"> client\_secret=:client\_secret&</span></span>

4

<span key="7c7ee3209480410597b27f0ef21a305a"><span offset-key="7c7ee3209480410597b27f0ef21a305a:0"> refresh\_token=:refresh\_token</span></span>

5

<span key="27eda11b18e84fe78f58d329db6c7bfe"><span offset-key="27eda11b18e84fe78f58d329db6c7bfe:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

6

<span key="f31cddebd439486aa523932962ed88f0"><span offset-key="f31cddebd439486aa523932962ed88f0:0">{</span></span>

7

<span key="968a74da83fc45298aef7869a6be3955"><span offset-key="968a74da83fc45298aef7869a6be3955:0"> "access\_token": &lt;TOKEN>,</span></span>

8

<span key="48d70bcd7ecd4f808debfe3d4aab8ccd"><span offset-key="48d70bcd7ecd4f808debfe3d4aab8ccd:0"> "expires\_in": &lt;EXPIRATION (in seconds)>,</span></span>

9

<span key="2f6746c3ed35472ca67565504edd1abe"><span offset-key="2f6746c3ed35472ca67565504edd1abe:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0yOTYzXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="6e7094acdb9c46228a5924992a618e1b"><span offset-key="6e7094acdb9c46228a5924992a618e1b:0">Figma files</span></span>

<span key="5e1d1e5ba7ec48d080e6eda6349d0792"><span offset-key="5e1d1e5ba7ec48d080e6eda6349d0792:0">Every file in Figma consists of a tree of nodes. At the root of every file is a DOCUMENT node, and from that node stems any CANVAS nodes. Every canvas node represents a PAGE in a Figma file. A canvas node can then have any number of nodes as its children. Each subtree stemming from a canvas node will represent a layer (e.g an object) on the canvas.</span></span>

<span key="93eff70e946b48aeaba45d1ab0903774"><span offset-key="93eff70e946b48aeaba45d1ab0903774:0">Nodes have a number of properties associated with them. Some of these are global properties, that exist on every node, whereas other node properties will be specific to the type of node.Global propertiesThe following are properties that exist on every node. These give us some basic information about identifying and viewing the node.</span></span>

Node type

Properties

<span key="85ffd04f37a74d95a17ea0f0466acda9"><span offset-key="85ffd04f37a74d95a17ea0f0466acda9:0">Node</span></span>

<span key="78478bc0168a401dbccbb2c8d1030ca7"><span offset-key="78478bc0168a401dbccbb2c8d1030ca7:0">idStringA string uniquely identifying this node within the document.nameStringThe name given to the node by the user in the tool.visibleBooleandefault: trueWhether or not the node is visible on the canvas.typeStringThe type of the node, refer to table below for details.pluginDataAnyData written by plugins that is visible only to the plugin that wrote it. Requires the \`pluginData\` to include the ID of the plugin.sharedPluginDataAnyData written by plugins that is visible to all plugins. Requires the \`pluginData\` parameter to include the string "shared".</span></span>

<span key="4f45a5f84eb144ec9bcd71638aab73f4"><span offset-key="4f45a5f84eb144ec9bcd71638aab73f4:0">Node typesNode type indicates what kind of node you are working with: for example, a FRAME node versus a RECTANGLE node. A node can have additional properties associated with it depending on its node type. The following is a catalog of properties that can be applied to a node, grouped by node type.</span></span>

Node type

Properties

<span key="fa69036324c0484c96707fd186b0d212"><span offset-key="fa69036324c0484c96707fd186b0d212:0">DOCUMENT</span></span>

<span key="b7062fc491624fe69ff260433b7c4ad6"><span offset-key="b7062fc491624fe69ff260433b7c4ad6:0">Property typesIn the section above, we gave you a brief description of the Node type and properties. offset-key="50ab35dc49db46ab872326690e700fa9:0">This field contains three vectors, each of which are a position in normalized object space (normalized object space is if the top left corner of the <span key="f9307fca22394b849284a843fdfb2241"><span offset-key="f9307fca22394b849284a843fdfb2241:0">EndpointsFiles endpoints allow for a wide range of functionality to get information about files. With a specific file key, you can get the JSON and image representations of the whole file or individual nodes within the file.GET file</span></span>

<span key="1870e7331e0444d4a6197d40f1125d62"><span offset-key="1870e7331e0444d4a6197d40f1125d62:0">Returns the document refered to by :key as a JSON object. The file key can be parsed from any Figma file url: https://www.figma.com/file/:key/:title. The name, lastModified, thumbnailUrl, editorType, and version attributes are all metadata of the retrieved file. The document attribute contains a Node of type </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#document-props" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="891647feb7504930a13005a9a434ae34" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="54907e93bea64217bbc230240788b1a3"><span data-offset-key="54907e93bea64217bbc230240788b1a3:0">DOCUMENT</span></span></span></a><span key="9f5951a9a6844b898c8fc3d30675a850"><span offset-key="9f5951a9a6844b898c8fc3d30675a850:0">. The components key contains a mapping from node IDs to component metadata. This is to help you determine which components each instance comes from.</span></span>

<span key="42987a95b27b481996e7b7d81591d3f2"><span offset-key="42987a95b27b481996e7b7d81591d3f2:0">HTTP Endpoint</span></span>

<span key="a2c98a12e68948ffbc7db982e7232910"><span offset-key="a2c98a12e68948ffbc7db982e7232910:0">GET/v1/files/:key</span></span>

Path parameters

Description

<span key="9f74faaccddb4115aeff54e2d15e9ee3"><span offset-key="9f74faaccddb4115aeff54e2d15e9ee3:0">key</span></span>

<span key="1c9e118ec5ad4c3b9338de770c58f3bc"><span offset-key="1c9e118ec5ad4c3b9338de770c58f3bc:0">StringFile to export JSON from</span></span>

Query parameters

Description

<span key="fbe7863ffd394d7bb070bc841156e75f"><span offset-key="fbe7863ffd394d7bb070bc841156e75f:0">version</span></span>

<span key="04ee371ade074e50b2cb85725aa88032"><span offset-key="04ee371ade074e50b2cb85725aa88032:0">StringoptionalA specific version ID to get. Omitting this will get the current version of the file</span></span>

<span key="9bfe45e5c0624a019cc20bdabb3afdbf"><span offset-key="9bfe45e5c0624a019cc20bdabb3afdbf:0">ids</span></span>

<span key="1d15ff4b945e4e3489c3ff5725312f50"><span offset-key="1d15ff4b945e4e3489c3ff5725312f50:0">StringoptionalComma separated list of nodes that you care about in the document. If specified, only a subset of the document will be returned corresponding to the nodes listed, their children, and everything between the root node and the listed nodes</span></span>

<span key="2617c1a1ca5d4cbab5b0fe2b4868cbb5"><span offset-key="2617c1a1ca5d4cbab5b0fe2b4868cbb5:0">depth</span></span>

<span key="1cb6b431765f464d83a748a013bbeeef"><span offset-key="1cb6b431765f464d83a748a013bbeeef:0">NumberoptionalPositive integer representing how deep into the document tree to traverse. For example, setting this to 1 returns only Pages, setting it to 2 returns Pages and all top level objects on each page. Not setting this parameter returns all nodes</span></span>

<span key="2b43e15ae4734412a641e963296dbb2f"><span offset-key="2b43e15ae4734412a641e963296dbb2f:0">GET file nodes</span></span>

<span key="d147f9bf4b1646a3826feec183644fcb"><span offset-key="d147f9bf4b1646a3826feec183644fcb:0">Returns the nodes referenced to by :ids as a JSON object. The nodes are retrieved from the Figma file referenced to by :key. The node Id and file key can be parsed from any Figma node url: https://www.figma.com/file/:key/:title?node-id=:id. The name, lastModified, thumbnailUrl, editorType, and version attributes are all metadata of the specified file. The document attribute contains a Node of type </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#document-props" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="121547ffad1344ecb36dd419ee5f9b54" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="190eaeecaa264236927c69410779e87e"><span data-offset-key="190eaeecaa264236927c69410779e87e:0">DOCUMENT</span></span></span></a><span key="19e34503255b4937bc16c1637fdf4372"><span offset-key="19e34503255b4937bc16c1637fdf4372:0">. The components key contains a mapping from node IDs to component metadata. This is to help you determine which components each instance comes from. By default, no vector data is returned. To return vector data, pass the geometry=paths parameter to the endpoint. Each node can also inherit properties from applicable styles. The styles key contains a mapping from style IDs to style metadata. Important: the nodes map may contain values that are null . This may be due to the node id not existing within the specified file.</span></span>

<span key="9d117b880e3b4aa29b552e1ffd9d55e4"><span offset-key="9d117b880e3b4aa29b552e1ffd9d55e4:0">GET image</span></span>

<span key="9d066af36a5e44849f250da9e90e411d"><span offset-key="9d066af36a5e44849f250da9e90e411d:0">Renders images from a file. If no error occurs, "images" will be populated with a map from node IDs to URLs of the rendered images, and "status" will be omitted. The image assets will expire after 30 days. Important: the image map may contain values that are null. This indicates that rendering of that specific node has failed. This may be due to the node id not existing, or other reasons such has the node having no renderable components. It is guaranteed that any node that was requested for rendering will be represented in this map whether or not the render succeeded.</span></span>

<span key="77ee4602f52d45ec9af5ba66f6df67b5"><span offset-key="77ee4602f52d45ec9af5ba66f6df67b5:0">GET image fills</span></span>

<span key="3ec9d03c06894714ab79c8ad79139637"><span offset-key="3ec9d03c06894714ab79c8ad79139637:0">Returns download links for all images present in image fills in a document. Image fills are how Figma represents any user supplied images. When you drag an image into Figma, we create a rectangle with a single fill that represents the image, and the user is able to transform the rectangle (and properties on the fill) as they wish. This endpoint returns a mapping from image references to the URLs at which the images may be download. Image URLs will expire after no more than 14 days. Image references are located in the output of the </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#files-endpoint" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5554c598736c4a3ba11bf40d2b8b24a7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="69f9f647ff4e4040b83d14445851098a"><span data-offset-key="69f9f647ff4e4040b83d14445851098a:0">GET files</span></span></span></a><span key="504d0e4dca7e4b6a901582a88cb9609c"><span offset-key="504d0e4dca7e4b6a901582a88cb9609c:0"> endpoint under the imageRef attribute in a </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#paint-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b4c15dfa16e446689c4732a0b1822c20" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="8a9af5d7aaf648f5905eea8b5bf910dc"><span data-offset-key="8a9af5d7aaf648f5905eea8b5bf910dc:0">Paint</span></span></span></a><span key="f45243ea67e447dda010924e31e0ea68"><span offset-key="f45243ea67e447dda010924e31e0ea68:0">.</span></span>

<span key="13a4f6254d3842cda913b19e514dc95e"><span offset-key="13a4f6254d3842cda913b19e514dc95e:0">CommentsFigma’s </span>*Commenting mode*<span offset-key="13a4f6254d3842cda913b19e514dc95e:2"> allows users to leave comments directly on layers or objects on the canvas. This is useful for collaboration when you want to suggest an adjustment, provide feedback, or critique a specific object or layout. You can use the Figma API to access a whole host of information about a comment, from when the comment was made and by whom, to its exact location on the canvas.TypesThere are a number of different properties associated with a comment, that help to give us more context. The following is a list of all the properties a comment will have:</span></span>

Type

Properties

<span key="315989f5e372476dbd9ff6648d12908a"><span offset-key="315989f5e372476dbd9ff6648d12908a:0">CommentA comment or reply left by a user</span></span>

<span key="551c8766c23142ffa6f0da2a4c63b474"><span offset-key="551c8766c23142ffa6f0da2a4c63b474:0">idStringUnique identifier for commentclient\_meta</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#vector-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e8417827b703491fb1e830f30ad7bad6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="f6be324b28e64d209224556734d30f69"><span data-offset-key="f6be324b28e64d209224556734d30f69:0">Vector</span></span></span></a><span key="e0cdc456d5714ffcb398b511a68dbceb"><span offset-key="e0cdc456d5714ffcb398b511a68dbceb:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#frameoffset-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="12dace8d2e084922a07e47b3c16b6a7c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="4bf9492bbc3d40d4818b7d7b311ebc4d"><span data-offset-key="4bf9492bbc3d40d4818b7d7b311ebc4d:0">FrameOffset</span></span></span></a><span key="7a7b5cb3c6574da6a6ab8d27c76ea1c1"><span offset-key="7a7b5cb3c6574da6a6ab8d27c76ea1c1:0">The position of the comment. Either the absolute coordinates on the canvas or a relative offset within a framefile\_keyStringThe file in which the comment livesparent\_idStringIf present, the id of the comment to which this is the replyuser</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#user-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bcc06a58f7824ff8a1dd3ca57f9d9e5e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="575cf4c5b4f44ca1aa1a9ea438d32dd2"><span data-offset-key="575cf4c5b4f44ca1aa1a9ea438d32dd2:0">User</span></span></span></a><span key="7cd07f128ebe4ca69a0388c217a3a182"><span offset-key="7cd07f128ebe4ca69a0388c217a3a182:0">The user who left the commentcreated\_atStringThe UTC ISO 8601 time at which the comment was leftresolved\_atStringIf set, the UTC ISO 8601 time the comment was resolvedorder\_idNumberOnly set for top level comments. The number displayed with the comment in the UI</span></span>

<span key="0e3d8e0e8a824955a8336404ff897e07"><span offset-key="0e3d8e0e8a824955a8336404ff897e07:0">EndpointsUnlike the other endpoints associated with the Figma API, you are able to </span>*post*<span offset-key="0e3d8e0e8a824955a8336404ff897e07:2"> comments to a Figma file - in addition to being able to view existing comments on a file. This means that there are both GET and POST endpoints available for comments.GET comments</span></span>

<span key="f5ecca8f63e746f29bd2c09cb9a3a26c"><span offset-key="f5ecca8f63e746f29bd2c09cb9a3a26c:0">Version historyFigma allows you to distinguish different stages or Versions of a file, as the file evolves over time. This is all recorded in the Version history, which allows users to view, track and restore previous versions of a File.TypesFigma will record some basic information about the file, like the who and when, as well as allow the user to determine a title and description for the version. These form the basis of the properties associated with version history.</span></span>

Type

<span key="ac8d40b7c54d49fba194d6e07a05bddd"><span offset-key="ac8d40b7c54d49fba194d6e07a05bddd:0">You can use this Endpoint to get a list of all the Projects within the specified team. This will only return projects visible to the authenticated user or owner of the developer token. Note: it is not currently possible to programmatically obtain the team id of a user just from a token. To obtain a team id, navigate to a team page of a team you are a part of. The team id will be present in the URL after the word team and before your team name.HTTP Endpoint</span></span>
