Copied!

<span key="7b9a518a0cfd4aaca5197cbc6fe9bb97"><span offset-key="7b9a518a0cfd4aaca5197cbc6fe9bb97:0">Webhooks V2Getting started</span></span>

<span key="8cad5bf13e1b4165a74d7c31b02be583"><span offset-key="8cad5bf13e1b4165a74d7c31b02be583:0">IMPORTANT: Webhooks V2 is still in open beta. Features and functions may change as we respond to feedback. Figma will attempt to keep APIs backwards compatible.</span></span>

<span key="0bfc484e4fd24c19a2054164a17c6180"><span offset-key="0bfc484e4fd24c19a2054164a17c6180:0">Webhooks allow you to observe when specific events happen in files. For example: a collaborator comments on a file, or you add a new version to a file's history. Using these events as triggers, you can build integrations with other applications. This can help to improve workflows, or extend the functionality of your design system.</span></span>

<span key="a3117f0481404750bbd916947a9998d6"><span offset-key="a3117f0481404750bbd916947a9998d6:0">Webhooks are attached to a specific team. All admins of that team can create and manage webhooks for the team. There is a limit of 20 webhooks per team. You can assign a certain event trigger to each webhook.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="b1b4c17b4aef4fa0a81764665910b26d"><span offset-key="b1b4c17b4aef4fa0a81764665910b26d:0">Webhooks will notify for files that are available to everyone on the team, or are in</span></span><a href="https://help.figma.com/hc/en-us/articles/360038512473" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8873d2bc07904577805dc60a2297b19f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="027f43512fcf4195961bc53cda17d1db"><span data-offset-key="027f43512fcf4195961bc53cda17d1db:0"> view-only projects</span></span></span></a><span key="119fd1b94f594dd29cb8f3d5466c0ee6"><span offset-key="119fd1b94f594dd29cb8f3d5466c0ee6:0">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d11f4b7f3e3444a4ac88c538af378747"><span offset-key="d11f4b7f3e3444a4ac88c538af378747:0">Webhooks will not notify for files in </span></span><a href="https://help.figma.com/hc/en-us/articles/360038512473" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3d2224aaee294ca882c66f919faf9ac4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="96c1fc07bf554b56921dc7e4d9c35131"><span data-offset-key="96c1fc07bf554b56921dc7e4d9c35131:0">invite-only projects.</span></span></span></a><span key="2920ec3750d04703a93e92ad8178800f"><span offset-key="2920ec3750d04703a93e92ad8178800f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="9cb8905c2c0b415ab3a833a3ff40532a"><span offset-key="9cb8905c2c0b415ab3a833a3ff40532a:0">Every payload (expect for PING) will contain the file name, file key and information related to the event triggered. This allows you to see which file triggered the event. Figma does not currently have an interface for webhooks. At the moment, you must create, modify, and delete webhooks through the webhooks API.</span></span>

<span key="0ab15cd4847641a6811edf216fd6424f"><span offset-key="0ab15cd4847641a6811edf216fd6424f:0">To get started with webhooks: Setup your local webserver and expose the endpoint Figma recommends using a tool similar to </span></span><a href="https://ngrok.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="468f579785c645109668d085e754956f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="f8a5ef7d75a34dfa800a85c7750b104c"><span data-offset-key="f8a5ef7d75a34dfa800a85c7750b104c:0">ngrok</span></span></span></a><span key="784aee26fbca43119220b3f790742615"><span offset-key="784aee26fbca43119220b3f790742615:0"> to expose a public URL for your local webserver. Configure your server to handle POST requests with a JSON payload Your server should return the status code 200 OK when it receives a webhook request. If it returns another status code, or takes too long, the Figma API will treat this as an error. Figma retries failed requests 3 times with an exponential backoff strategy.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="c11445f639e0462280ab320500fc2ca4"><span offset-key="c11445f639e0462280ab320500fc2ca4:0">The first retry occurs 5 minutes after the first failure.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="aebb986b30e04ecf90cf3663742691bf"><span offset-key="aebb986b30e04ecf90cf3663742691bf:0">The second retry occurs 30 minutes after the second failure.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="6b074d60687547648b5575aff5b73e11"><span offset-key="6b074d60687547648b5575aff5b73e11:0">The final retry occurs 3 hours after the third failure.</span></span>

<span key="a2a02a8a9ed546c3b78ffa6fb18ff570"><span offset-key="a2a02a8a9ed546c3b78ffa6fb18ff570:0">Figma does not currently deactivate endpoints with frequent errors. Create your webhook Use the </span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#webhooks-v2-post-endpoint" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="03025af066fa43c4b610370a8b621e09" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="689dc289f42f49809f8fcc88d67be14c"><span data-offset-key="689dc289f42f49809f8fcc88d67be14c:0">POST Webhook</span></span></span></a><span key="64d315b672b4488d84e06dccdbd4de69"><span offset-key="64d315b672b4488d84e06dccdbd4de69:0"> endpoint to attach a webhook to a team. You will need to be an admin of the team to create a webhook. If you are successful, you will receive a PING event. This means your webhook is working and will receive any updates.</span></span>

<span key="c510b53729be4ae8af40bc3f026cbe95"><span offset-key="c510b53729be4ae8af40bc3f026cbe95:0">If you are having problems with your webhook, you can query the</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#webhooks-v2-requests-endpoint" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b11c4d34c63748549f92c6c762b3cd91" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="d795ca061a09489297415aa37b2ce5de"><span data-offset-key="d795ca061a09489297415aa37b2ce5de:0">webhook requests endpoint</span></span></span></a><span key="733e0c28039f4771ab9a5ced9a8d2329"><span offset-key="733e0c28039f4771ab9a5ced9a8d2329:0">. This will list all requests and responses within the past seven days.Events</span></span>

Event name

Trigger condition

<span key="769d5f3d448148f497b01694f9c9dbd0"><span offset-key="769d5f3d448148f497b01694f9c9dbd0:0">PING</span></span>

<span key="053219a23a18401fbd55233b8d09d83e"><span offset-key="053219a23a18401fbd55233b8d09d83e:0">Triggers when a webhook is created. Used for debugging. Cannot be subscribed to, all webhooks will recieve PING events.</span></span>

<span key="8834f435e1b94338a9f86c46b5b6901d"><span offset-key="8834f435e1b94338a9f86c46b5b6901d:0">FILE\_UPDATE</span></span>

<span key="900e84494fc44c3e97c03218c15e12fe"><span offset-key="900e84494fc44c3e97c03218c15e12fe:0">Triggers whenever a file saves. This occurs whenever a file is closed or within 30 seconds after changes have been made.</span></span>

<span key="ec4134f0f933442ea919cf7d97a5979c"><span offset-key="ec4134f0f933442ea919cf7d97a5979c:0">FILE\_VERSION\_UPDATE</span></span>

<span key="d8341eb6f8d94397b34572b209ffc081"><span offset-key="d8341eb6f8d94397b34572b209ffc081:0">Triggers whenever a named version is created in the version history of a file.</span></span>

<span key="1a00622484e148d49ac77b36e49026b9"><span offset-key="1a00622484e148d49ac77b36e49026b9:0">FILE\_DELETE</span></span>

<span key="cbb0651bfafc4c43bd9d177240001d2c"><span offset-key="cbb0651bfafc4c43bd9d177240001d2c:0">Triggers whenever a file has been deleted. If you subscribe to FILE\_UPDATE, you automatically get these notifications. Note that this does not trigger on all files within a folder, if the folder is deleted.</span></span>

<span key="87af55e21e1e4f8682d58bbadaeecb8f"><span offset-key="87af55e21e1e4f8682d58bbadaeecb8f:0">LIBRARY\_PUBLISH</span></span>

<span key="79e47d2faa7e4a08bde5459c91c2ab57"><span offset-key="79e47d2faa7e4a08bde5459c91c2ab57:0">Triggers whenever a library file is published.</span></span>

<span key="f00571b3c7f6441b97055f7ddc87b8b5"><span offset-key="f00571b3c7f6441b97055f7ddc87b8b5:0">FILE\_COMMENT</span></span>

<span key="160c5dee44d64c3cb7d3c8f8dc2e097a"><span offset-key="160c5dee44d64c3cb7d3c8f8dc2e097a:0">Triggers when someone comments on a file.</span></span>

<span key="7fa2a44ab1374be88fd5f31fa70090bf"><span offset-key="7fa2a44ab1374be88fd5f31fa70090bf:0">Payloads</span></span>

Type

Properties

<span key="8735546a40a549b890e5405d4b870288"><span offset-key="8735546a40a549b890e5405d4b870288:0">PING</span></span>

<span key="d0a1228cc8fc4aa8ad34346dd313a272"><span offset-key="d0a1228cc8fc4aa8ad34346dd313a272:0">Debug event triggered whenever a webhook is created. Use this to verify that your endpoint was setup correctly.event\_typeStringThe type of event that triggered this webhook callpasscodeStringThe passcode specified when the webhook was created, should match what was initially providedtimestampStringUTC ISO 8601 timestamp of when the event was triggered.webhook\_idNumberThe id of the webhook that caused the callback> Example</span></span>

<span key="08656bb048884a15abcac88ab0724225"><span offset-key="08656bb048884a15abcac88ab0724225:0">FILE\_UPDATE</span></span>

<span key="76d4171e7a604ed8ac88c170f30c996b"><span offset-key="76d4171e7a604ed8ac88c170f30c996b:0">Triggers whenever a file is saved. This occurs if a file is closed or within 30 seconds after changes are made.</span></span>

<span key="0bd05b64301d4a85865cdea2a5abefbf"><span offset-key="0bd05b64301d4a85865cdea2a5abefbf:0">This is useful when you want to stay up-to-date with the contents of a file. For example, you could generate a static website from your Figma document and keep it always up-to-date with this webhook.event\_typeStringThe type of event that triggered this webhook callfile\_keyStringThe key of the file that was updatedfile\_nameStringThe name of the file that was updatedpasscodeStringThe passcode specified when the webhook was created, should match what was initially providedtimestampStringUTC ISO 8601 timestamp of when the event was triggered.webhook\_idNumberThe id of the webhook that caused the callback> Example</span></span>

<span key="e6c138d5aa8d4594aeece181d79419aa"><span offset-key="e6c138d5aa8d4594aeece181d79419aa:0">FILE\_DELETE</span></span>

<span key="7089f743865041f1b63be25c9b20721b"><span offset-key="7089f743865041f1b63be25c9b20721b:0">Triggers whenever a file is trashed. Note if a folder is deleted, this event will not trigger for files within the folder.</span></span>

<span key="c7f70717b4c14104b512eb90e194b48e"><span offset-key="c7f70717b4c14104b512eb90e194b48e:0">This event will also be sent out to webhooks that subscribe to FILE\_UPDATE.event\_typeStringThe type of event that triggered this webhook callfile\_keyStringThe key of the file that was updatedfile\_nameStringThe name of the file that was updatedpasscodeStringThe passcode specified when the webhook was created, should match what was initially providedtimestampStringUTC ISO 8601 timestamp of when the event was triggered.triggered\_by</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#user-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6175869124a4465e9f9583c22fc0ab26" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="700b087dfa88470696131a8fad4b8e4d"><span data-offset-key="700b087dfa88470696131a8fad4b8e4d:0">User</span></span></span></a><span key="7cd922078cb24a1ba41f77a7e7d0a975"><span offset-key="7cd922078cb24a1ba41f77a7e7d0a975:0">The user that deleted the file and triggered this eventwebhook\_idNumberThe id of the webhook that caused the callback> Example</span></span>

<span key="7410f6f816484218a4d72a2161321f9a"><span offset-key="7410f6f816484218a4d72a2161321f9a:0">FILE\_VERSION\_UPDATE</span></span>

<span key="b4fdba1b03a141b1a2b9149505163a65"><span offset-key="b4fdba1b03a141b1a2b9149505163a65:0">Triggers whenever a user creates a named version in the version history of a file.</span></span>

<span key="38fbbb2616694b8bb099922a4dd08d73"><span offset-key="38fbbb2616694b8bb099922a4dd08d73:0">This is useful for workflow integrations. For example, suppose you have a Figma document with icon assets. When the design for an asset is updated and ready to publish, you can have a member of the team tag that version in the version history and then use this webhook event to generate and deploy your new asset version.created\_atStringUTC ISO 8601 timestamp of when the version was createddescriptionStringDesciption of the version in the version historyevent\_typeStringThe type of event that triggered this webhook callfile\_keyStringThe key of the file that was updatedfile\_nameStringThe name of the file that was updatedlabelStringLable of the version in the version historypasscodeStringThe passcode specified when the webhook was created, should match what was initially providedtimestampStringUTC ISO 8601 timestamp of when the event was triggeredtriggered\_by</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#user-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="83e4ca10456b4d50bfe31671343e5a00" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="4adde002f3154e50a4f39b99fa6b4fd6"><span data-offset-key="4adde002f3154e50a4f39b99fa6b4fd6:0">User</span></span></span></a><span key="21a790cdab4c440d8b18f5361df688a4"><span offset-key="21a790cdab4c440d8b18f5361df688a4:0">The user that created the named version and triggered this eventversion\_idStringId of the published versionwebhook\_idNumberThe id of the webhook that caused the callback> Example</span></span>

<span key="13abecdb2f884ca5bf76349819ab9b55"><span offset-key="13abecdb2f884ca5bf76349819ab9b55:0">LIBRARY\_PUBLISH</span></span>

<span key="3c77ccacf87540ad83e5b8c215fdad3a"><span offset-key="3c77ccacf87540ad83e5b8c215fdad3a:0">Triggers whenever a user publishes a library file.</span></span>

<span key="74e8f60b554b48cd9269702c6f14aea3"><span offset-key="74e8f60b554b48cd9269702c6f14aea3:0">This is useful for workflow integrations. This webhook could integrate with Slack, Asana or Jira, notifying designers to modify their assets when new components are published.created\_components</span></span><a <span key="c5ae2f98fc764942bcde44fa99dbe5d8"><span offset-key="c5ae2f98fc764942bcde44fa99dbe5d8:0">FILE\_COMMENT</span></span>

<span key="3f360c37938649ad9cb950eb69d2d6e9"><span offset-key="3f360c37938649ad9cb950eb69d2d6e9:0">Triggers whenever a user comments on a file.</span></span>

<span key="159050105fbf40369bcb9b6943c4a446"><span offset-key="159050105fbf40369bcb9b6943c4a446:0">This webhook could integrate with Asana or Jira and automatically create tasks whenever a user comments. It could also integrate with Slack and notify mentioned users.</span></span>

<span key="bb3a9fa03c4147bf81fe485c050c13c8"><span offset-key="bb3a9fa03c4147bf81fe485c050c13c8:0">The contents of a comment is returned in an array of CommentFragment. A CommentFragment either contains a text of mention field. A text field contains raw comment text with formatting derivatives, newlines will be encoded as \\n, etc. Text fields can also contain emojis, which are always encoded as a separate fragment and are surrounded by two : characters. Mention fields occur if a user types @OtherUser in their comment. A mention contains the userid of the mentioned user. All mentioned users are added to the mentioned array field, where additional user information is included.comment</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#commentfragment-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="212ae105b84d4708bcb9ac818c15cd88" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="1a1faaa9debc40a88a08c8f287cb599e"><span data-offset-key="1a1faaa9debc40a88a08c8f287cb599e:0">CommentFragment[]</span></span></span></a><span key="505fd45b992542c8b5c0e10c7d9ab5cf"><span offset-key="505fd45b992542c8b5c0e10c7d9ab5cf:0">Contents of the comment itselfcomment\_idNumberUnique identifier for commentcreated\_atStringThe UTC ISO 8601 time at which the comment was leftevent\_typeStringThe type of event that triggered this webhook callfile\_keyStringThe key of the file that was updatedfile\_nameStringThe name of the file that was updatedmentions</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#user-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d269df7232ba4e9087a0da2bdc2e11aa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="a3c938f3b9014b46aa027b2d09846c72"><span data-offset-key="a3c938f3b9014b46aa027b2d09846c72:0">User[]</span></span></span></a><span key="5cceccbf0d374f9ba8cd1e7c78370e6b"><span offset-key="5cceccbf0d374f9ba8cd1e7c78370e6b:0">Users that were mentioned in the commentorder\_idNumberOnly set for top level comments. The number displayed with the comment in the UIparent\_idNumberIf present, the id of the comment to which this is the replypasscodeStringThe passcode specified when the webhook was created, should match what was initially providedresolved\_atStringIf set, the UTC ISO 8601 time the comment was resolvedtimestampStringUTC ISO 8601 timestamp of when the event was triggeredtriggered\_by</span></span><a href="https://www.figma.com/developers/api#user-type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1704899e9d1346bf870896290fccc677" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-2959_259-2960-237__"><span data-key="673ef60e9d834b9d8d4a413ddafdeba5"><span data-offset-key="673ef60e9d834b9d8d4a413ddafdeba5:0">User</span></span></span></a><span key="af5471eb73ff45d8a4420babc06a4bd6"><span offset-key="af5471eb73ff45d8a4420babc06a4bd6:0">The user that made the comment and triggered the event> Example</span></span>

<span key="353ff8eeacb9443e92471c084adb1ca9"><span offset-key="353ff8eeacb9443e92471c084adb1ca9:0">Security</span></span>

## 

<span key="485fbe1f292a44aa87270f4082a0955c"><span offset-key="485fbe1f292a44aa87270f4082a0955c:0">Securing your webhook</span></span>

<span key="2161b32909cb406c921361436ee09f3b"><span offset-key="2161b32909cb406c921361436ee09f3b:0">IMPORTANT: When creating a webhook you are required to pass in a passcode. The purpose of the passcode field is so that your application can verify that Figma is actually what is calling your endpoint (as opposed to some attacker trying to make you believe something about your users' Figma files).</span></span>

<span key="573bf8a4badc4b228a4dd76b528efeeb"><span offset-key="573bf8a4badc4b228a4dd76b528efeeb:0">We would recommend comparing the passcode we pass back to you with the passcode originally provided when creating the endpoint to make sure they match before acting on the webhook trigger. If you receive a request with the wrong passcode, you should respond with a 400 Bad Request HTTP response which will immediately stop the webhook.Errors</span></span>

<span key="11f6b0a49b8848efbae04ffacd917cb7"><span offset-key="11f6b0a49b8848efbae04ffacd917cb7:0">This section outlines the common error codes and resolutions you may encounter while using the Figma API.</span></span>

Error code

Description

<span key="96ed53025f6f430cbe2970a9e5260f64"><span offset-key="96ed53025f6f430cbe2970a9e5260f64:0">400Bad request</span></span>

<span key="80fa3ee89bb24390b63e7234f1c0a289"><span offset-key="80fa3ee89bb24390b63e7234f1c0a289:0">Parameters are invalid or malformed. Please check the input formats.</span></span>

<span key="7da530a4467340428ac67e719d1f4739"><span offset-key="7da530a4467340428ac67e719d1f4739:0">404Not found</span></span>

<span key="b3ff1f0fc8274086a10977adaff19970"><span offset-key="b3ff1f0fc8274086a10977adaff19970:0">The requested file or resource was not found.</span></span>

<span key="77ac15f117934e28ba0cf57af5aed0f4"><span offset-key="77ac15f117934e28ba0cf57af5aed0f4:0">429Rate limit</span></span>

<span key="6946569c77ad47df807080d7e94b2cbe"><span offset-key="6946569c77ad47df807080d7e94b2cbe:0">In some cases API requests may be throttled or rate limited. Please wait a while before attempting the request again (typically a minute).</span></span>

<span key="5132cf1811f745fc9b6f238b7ea0f5e0"><span offset-key="5132cf1811f745fc9b6f238b7ea0f5e0:0">500Internal server error</span></span>

<span key="c2802ebd72b84439b190f008248efabb"><span offset-key="c2802ebd72b84439b190f008248efabb:0">This most commonly occurs for very large image render requests, which may time out our server and return a 500. Please reduce the number and size of objects requested.</span></span>
